    AND c.id_ciudad = o.id_ciudad
    AND p.id_provincia = c.id_provincia
    AND os.id_ofertas = o.id_ofertas
    AND j.id_jornada = o.id_jornada
    AND p.id_pais = 39 AND (o.estado = 1 OR o.estado = 2 OR o.estado = 3) AND o.id_empresa IN(1) AND o.id_empresa = emp.id_empresa AND ul.id_usuario_login = emp.id_usuario_login GROUP BY o.id_ofertas ORDER BY orden_urgente DESC,o.fecha_creado DESC LIMIT 0,20

                   GROUP_CONCAT(a.descripcion ORDER BY e.orden) AS permisos,
                   GROUP_CONCAT(a.accion ORDER BY e.orden) AS acciones
            FROM mfo_plan p

            INNER JOIN mfo_accionsist a ON e.id_accionSist = a.id_accionSist            
            WHERE p.tipo_usuario = '1' AND p.estado = 1 AND p.id_sucursal = '1' AND
